        <script type="text/javascript">
            (function() {
                /* move share to top */
                /*
                var socialWrapper = $('#new-social-share');
                socialWrapper.attr('style',socialWrapper.attr('style') + ';z-index:99');
                */
                /* process share links */
                var sharelinks = $('#new-social-share > .share-icons > li > a');
                var log = function log(item) {
                    if (window.logdebug && console && console.log) {
                        console.log(item);
                    }
                }
                function hideprint(items) {
                    log("hide print");
                    if (!window.print) {
                        log('no JS print functionality available');
                        items.filter('.print').parent().hide();
                    }
                }
                var sharepop = function sharepop(item) {
                    log("share pop");
                    var url = item.url;
                    var sharetext = item.sharetext;
                    var additionaltext = item.additionaltext;
                    var currentpage = encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);
                    url = url.replace('[text]', sharetext + ' ');
                    url = url.replace('[additionaltext]', additionaltext);
                    url = url.replace('[pagetitle]', document.title.replace("|", " - "));
                    url += currentpage;
                    log("url: "+url);
                    var newWin = window.open(url);
                }
                var sharefunc = function sharefunc() {
                    log('share func');
                    var link = $(this);
                    log(link);
                    var linkType = link.attr('class').replace('icon-social ', '');
                    log('Link type: ' + linkType);
                    switch (linkType) {
                    case 'facebook':
                        sharepop({
                            'url': 'https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=',
                            'sharetext': '',
                            'additionaltext': ''
                        });
                        break;
                    case 'twitter':
                        sharepop({
                            'url': 'https://twitter.com/home?status=[text]',
                            'sharetext': link.attr('sharetext'),
                            'additionaltext': ''
                        });
                        break;
                        case 'in':
                            sharepop({
                                'url': 'https://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&title=[additionaltext]&summary=[text]&source=[pagetitle]&url=',
                                'sharetext': link.attr('sharetext'),
                                'additionaltext': link.attr('additionaltext')
                            });
                            break;
                        case 'gplus':
                            sharepop({
                                'url': 'https://plus.google.com/share?url=',
                                'sharetext': '',
                                'additionaltext': ''
                            });
                            break;
                        case 'print':
                        if (window.print) {
                            log("printing");
                            window.print();
                        }
                        break;
                    case 'mail':
                        sharepop({
                            'url': 'mailto:?subject=[additionaltext]&body=[text]',
                            'sharetext': link.attr('sharetext'),
                            'additionaltext': link.attr('additionaltext')
                        });
                        break;
						
						default:
						alert(' social icon not supported');
						break;
                    }
                    return false;
                }
                hideprint(sharelinks);
                sharelinks.on('click', sharefunc);
            })();

          if(functionalIdsValue == null || functionalIdsValue.length == 0){
            return '';
          }
